# Description_Notes_and_Keywords
#   Description: Samples collected for various history-related reasons during the last two decades, and grouped to represent two different altitudes (Grangarde [SWED335] 155-250m, and Safsnas [SWED336] 300-480m). The trees react on T and P signals in a complex way in this area; the lower altitude group correlates better towards southern Scandinavia and the higher better towards north. NOAA Template Raw Measurements file added 2021-02-22.
